230 	public static final String[] tokenNames;
231 	static {
232 		tokenNames = new String[_SYMBOLIC_NAMES.length];
233 		for (int i = 0; i < tokenNames.length; i++) {
234 			tokenNames[i] = VOCABULARY.getLiteralName(i);
235 			if (tokenNames[i] == null) {
236 				tokenNames[i] = VOCABULARY.getSymbolicName(i);
237 			}
238 
239 			if (tokenNames[i] == null) {
240 				tokenNames[i] = "<INVALID>";
241 			}
242 		}
243 	}
